NOTICE ...

NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICE
TO WHOMSOEVER IT MAY CONCERN
Pastor Farly Wilson Joseph Pillai the Chief Pastor of The Pentecostal Mission has expired on 3rd March 2014.
The Deputy Chief Pastor, Pastor Geoffrey Sam Peter has succeeded him as the Chief Pastor on the same date as per
the Nomination, dated 9th November 2006.
Pastor Geoffrey Sam Peter will hereafter be the President cum Treasurer of the Society and the Chief Pastor of the
Mission in India, Australia, Canada, Colombia, Congo, Costa Rica, Cyprus, Dominican Republic, E1 Salvador, Fiji, France,
Gambia, Germany, Ghana, Guadeloupe, Gulf Countries, Honduras, Hong Kong, Jamaica, Kenya, Malawi, Malaysia, Mauritius,
Mexico, Nepal, New Zealand, Nicaragua, Nigeria, Philippines, P.N.G., Puerto Rico, Seychelles, Sierra Leone, Singapore,
Sri Lanka, Switzerland, Togo, Trinidad & Tobago, U.K., U.S.A., and in any other countries wherever the work may be extended.

Chennai-600 063
28th March 2014.

PASTOR GEOFFREY SAM PETER
The Pentecostal Mission
Chief Pastor.

ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
